behavior find_clothes_shirt_2158_around_basket_for_clothes_2078(clothes_shirt:item):

    body:

            is_basket_for_clothes(basket_for_clothes_instance) and id[basket_for_clothes_instance]==2078
        achieve close_char(char,basket_for_clothes_instance)
        if can_open(basket_for_clothes_instance):

            exp(clothes_shirt,basket_for_clothes_instance)
        else:
            exp(clothes_shirt,basket_for_clothes_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[clothes_shirt]=False
        close[clothes_shirt,basket_for_clothes_instance]=True
        close[basket_for_clothes_instance,clothes_shirt]=True

#goal_representation
 
behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item, faucet:item, soap:item):
    body:
        achieve has_water(shirt)
        # Fill the shirt with water
        wash(shirt)
        # Wash the shirt with water
        if is_soap(soap):
            achieve_once inhand(soap)
            scrub(shirt)
            # Scrub the shirt using soap
            achieve_once inhand(soap)
        rinse(shirt)
        # Rinse the shirt with clean water
        squeeze(shirt)
        # Squeeze excess water from the shirt
        achieve clean(shirt)
        # Ensure shirt is completely clean

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve plugged(iron)
        # Plug in the iron
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Turn on the iron
        observe(iron,"Is the iron ready for use")
        # Check if the iron is ready for use
        achieve clean(shirt)
        # Ensure the shirt is clean before ironing
        achieve_once inhand(iron)
        # Take the iron in hand
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Iron the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve_once unplugged(iron)
        # Unplug the iron once ironing is complete
        achieve clean(shirt)
        # Shirt remains clean after ironing

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        # Bind a shirt item
        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet)
        # Bind a faucet for water
        bind soap: item where:
            is_soap(soap)
        # Bind a soap item
        wash_shirt(shirt, faucet, soap)
        
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron)
        # Bind an iron item
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Bind an ironing board
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, ironing_board)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item, soap:item):
    body:
        wash(shirt) # Wash the shirt with water
        scrub(shirt) # Scrub the shirt using soap
        rinse(shirt) # Rinse the soap off the shirt
        squeeze(shirt) # Squeeze water from the shirt
        achieve clean(shirt) # Ensure the shirt is clean

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, board) # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve plugged(iron) # Plug in the iron
        achieve is_on(iron) # Turn on the iron
        achieve clean(shirt) # Ensure the shirt is clean before ironing
        achieve_once inhand(iron) # Temporarily hold the iron by the handle
        achieve_once on(shirt, board) # Ensure the shirt stays on the board during ironing

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) # Select a shirt instance
        bind soap: item where:
            is_soap(soap) # Select soap
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) # Select an iron
        bind board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(board) # Select an ironing board
        wash_shirt(shirt, soap) # Wash the shirt
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, board) # Iron the shirt after washing

#goal_representation_end

behavior find_detergent_2155_around_cupboard_117(detergent:item):
    goal: not unknown(detergent)
    body:
        assert is_detergent(detergent)
        bind cupboard_instance:item where:
            is_cupboard(cupboard_instance) and id[cupboard_instance]==117
        achieve close_char(char,cupboard_instance)
        if can_open(cupboard_instance):
            achieve_once open(cupboard_instance)
            exp(detergent,cupboard_instance)
        else:
            exp(detergent,cupboard_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[detergent]=False
        close[detergent,cupboard_instance]=True
        close[cupboard_instance,detergent]=True

#goal_representation
 
behavior hand_wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        wash(shirt)
        # Wash the shirt by hand
        rinse(shirt)
        # Rinse the shirt
        squeeze(shirt)
        # Squeeze the shirt to remove excess water

behavior iron_clothes(clothing:item, iron:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(clothing, ironing_board) 
        # Place the clothing on the ironing board
        achieve plugged(iron) 
        # Ensure the iron is plugged in
        achieve is_on(iron) 
        # Turn the iron on
        achieve_once close_char(char, ironing_board)
        # Move the character close to the ironing board

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        # Bind a shirt for washing and ironing tasks

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron)
        # Select an iron

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Select an ironing board

        hand_wash_shirt(shirt)
        # Execute the hand washing behavior for the shirt
        
        iron_clothes(shirt, iron, ironing_board)
        # Execute the ironing behavior for the shirt

#goal_representation_end

    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        # Plug in the iron
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Turn on the iron
        achieve clean(shirt)
        # Ensure the shirt is clean and ironed

#goal_representation

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(shirt)
        achieve has_water(shirt)

behavior rinse_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(shirt)
        achieve_once has_water(shirt) # Release has_water status after rinsing

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, board)
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        achieve is_on(iron)

def get_iron(cupboard:item):
    foreach o: item:
        if is_iron(o) and close(o, cupboard):
            return o

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        # Select the shirt you want to hand wash

        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet)
        # Select the faucet

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Select the ironing board

        bind cupboard: item where:
            is_cupboard(cupboard)
        # Select the cupboard from the correct ID

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and iron == get_iron(cupboard)
        # Select iron

        wash_shirt(shirt)
        rinse_shirt(shirt)
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, ironing_board)

        wash(item)
        rinse(item)

behavior iron_clothes(clothing: item, location: item, iron: item):
    body:
        achieve close_char(char, iron)
        achieve_once inhand(iron)
        achieve close_char(char, location)
        achieve on(clothing, location)

#goal_representation
 
def in_handwashing_area(faucet:item):
    # Function to check if faucet is in the handwashing area
    # No specific handwashing_area category is defined, checking based on faucet is plausible
    return is_faucet(faucet)

def determine_cleanliness(shirt:item):
    # Function to check if a shirt is clean
    symbol clean_status = not dirty(shirt)
    return clean_status

behavior hand_wash_shirt(shirt:item, faucet:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(faucet) # Turn on the faucet to start washing
        wash(shirt) # Wash the shirt at the faucet
        achieve_once has_water(shirt) # Ensure the shirt has water, indicating its been washed
        achieve_once is_off(faucet) # Turn off the faucet once done

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, board) # Ensure shirt is on the ironing board
        achieve_once plugged(iron) # Plug in the iron to start ironing
        achieve_once is_on(iron) # Turn on the iron
        # Ironing would be an implicit goal under achieve_once because its not manually defined
        achieve_once is_off(iron) # Turn off the iron after use

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and not determine_cleanliness(shirt)
        # Bind the item that is a shirt and dirty
        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet) and in_handwashing_area(faucet)
        # Bind the item that is a faucet in typical handwashing area
        hand_wash_shirt(shirt, faucet)

        bind board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(board)
        # Bind the item that is an ironing board
        foreach iron_o: item:
            if is_iron(iron_o) and not visited(iron_o):
                observe(iron_o, "Inspect if its operational")
                # Find a usable iron
                bind iron: item where:
                    is_iron(iron)
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, board)

#goal_representation_end

def in_basket_for_clothes(shirt:item, basket:item):
    # Function to check if the shirt is in the specified basket for clothes
    symbol is_inside_basket= exists o: item : (is_clothes_shirt(o) and inside(o, basket))
    return is_inside_basket

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve_once clean(shirt)
        # Hand wash the shirt until it is clean

behavior rinse_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve_once has_water(shirt)
        # Rinse the shirt to ensure it has water on it

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, board)
        # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        # Ensure the iron is plugged in

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select a basket for clothes
        
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and in_basket_for_clothes(shirt, basket)
        # Select a shirt that is in the basket

        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet)
        # Select a faucet

        bind board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(board)
        # Select an ironing board

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron)
        wash_shirt(shirt)
        rinse_shirt(shirt)
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, board)

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item, sink:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(shirt, sink)
        wash(shirt)
        rinse(shirt)

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, ironing_board:item, powersocket:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve plugged(iron)
        achieve_once is_on(iron)
        push(iron)
        pull(iron)
        achieve_once unplugged(iron)

behavior find_and_wash_shirt(sink:item):
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        achieve_once close_char(char, shirt)
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        wash_shirt(shirt, sink)

        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        achieve_once close_char(char, shirt)
        bind ironing_board: item where:

            is_iron(iron)
        bind powersocket: item where:
            is_powersocket(powersocket)

            is_iron(iron)

def is_clothes_shirt_clean(shirt:item):
    # Function to check if the shirt is clean
    symbol shirt_clean = clean(shirt)
    return shirt_clean

def has_water_sink(sink:item):
    # Function to check if the sink has water
    symbol sink_has_water = has_water(sink)
    return sink_has_water

behavior hand_wash(shirt:item, sink:item):
    body:
        achieve_once clean(shirt)
        # Hand wash the shirt to make it clean

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, ironing_board:item, iron:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Place the shirt on the ironing board and iron it

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and not is_clothes_shirt_clean(shirt)
        # Select the dirty shirt
        
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink) and has_water_sink(sink)
        # Select a sink with water

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Select an ironing board

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and plugged(iron) and is_off(iron)
        # Select a plugged but powered off iron

        hand_wash(shirt, sink) # Wash the shirt in the sink
        iron_shirt(shirt, ironing_board, iron) # Iron the washed shirt

behavior find_detergent_2011_around_washing_machine_2079(detergent:item):
    goal: not unknown(detergent)
    body:
        assert is_detergent(detergent)
        bind washing_machine_instance:item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine_instance) and id[washing_machine_instance]==2079
        achieve close_char(char,washing_machine_instance)
        if can_open(washing_machine_instance):
            achieve_once open(washing_machine_instance)
            exp(detergent,washing_machine_instance)
        else:
            exp(detergent,washing_machine_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[detergent]=False
        close[detergent,washing_machine_instance]=True
        close[washing_machine_instance,detergent]=True

#goal_representation
 
behavior hand_wash_shirt(shirt:item, sink:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(shirt)
        achieve has_water(sink)

behavior prepare_ironing_board(shirt:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)

behavior find_and_prepare_iron(iron:item, bowl:item):
    body:
        achieve visited(iron)
        achieve close_char(char, iron)
        observe(iron, "Check if it has a switch and is movable")
        achieve_once on(iron, bowl)

behavior ironing_shirt(iron:item, shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(iron)
        achieve_once close_char(char, shirt)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
            
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and id[bowl] == 2142

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron] == 2161

        hand_wash_shirt(shirt, sink)
        prepare_ironing_board(shirt, ironing_board)
        find_and_prepare_iron(iron, bowl)
        ironing_shirt(iron, shirt)

#goal_representation
 
def find_iron_in_dining_room(dining_room: item):
    # Function to locate the iron inside the dining room
    symbol found_iron= exists bowl: item : (is_bowl(bowl) and inside(bowl, dining_room) and on(iron, bowl))
    return found_iron

behavior retrieve_iron(iron: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inhand(iron)

behavior hand_wash_shirt(shirt: item, sink: item):
    body:
        achieve has_water(sink) # Ensure the sink has water
        achieve clean(shirt) # Clean the shirt
        # Rinse the shirt to ensure it is free of detergent or soap
        rinse(shirt)

behavior iron_shirt(shirt: item, iron: item, ironing_board: item):
    body:
        achieve_once plugged(iron) # Plug the iron in
        achieve_once is_on(iron) # Turn on the iron
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board) # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve clean(shirt) # The shirt should remain clean

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room]==41
        # Select dining_room_41

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron]==2161
        # Select iron_2161

        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        # Bind the sink for washing

        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and id[shirt]==2158
        # Select clothes_shirt_2158

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Bind the ironing board for ironing

        if not find_iron_in_dining_room(dining_room):
            # Verify if the iron is found in the dining room
            observe(dining_room, "Look for iron inside the dining room and check its location on the bowl")

        retrieve_iron(iron)
        hand_wash_shirt(shirt, sink)
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, ironing_board)

#goal_representation_end

def find_iron_2161():
    # Function to check if iron_2161 is located on a specific bowl in dining_room_41
    bind dining_room: item where:
        is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room]==41
    bind bowl: item where:
        is_bowl(bowl) and id[bowl]==2142 and inside(bowl, dining_room)
    return exists iron: item : (is_iron(iron) and id[iron]==2161 and on(iron, bowl))

behavior retrieve_iron_2161():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room]==41
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and id[bowl]==2142 and inside(bowl, dining_room)
        if find_iron_2161():
            # Iron has already been located in the dining room
            bind iron: item where:
                is_iron(iron) and id[iron]==2161 and on(iron, bowl)
            # Ensure the character is close to the bowl containing the iron
            achieve close_char(char, bowl)
        else:
            # If not found, additional observation is needed
            observe(bowl, "Check if iron_2161 is on bowl_2142")

behavior iron_shirt(iron:item, shirt:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve close_char(char, ironing_board)
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        achieve_once is_on(iron)
        achieve_once on(iron, shirt)
        pull(iron)   # Simulating the ironing action
        push(iron)   # Simulating the ironing action
        achieve_once is_off(iron) # Turn off iron after use

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and id[shirt]==2158
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board) and id[ironing_board]==2144
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron]==2161
        retrieve_iron_2161()
        achieve clean(shirt) # Ensure the shirt is clean
        iron_shirt(iron, shirt, ironing_board)

def locate_iron(dining_room:item):
    # Check if the bowl with the iron on top is visited or not
    foreach b: item:
        if is_bowl(b) and not visited(b) and inside(b, dining_room):
            observe(b, "Find iron on the bowl")
            # Observe the bowl to check if the iron is on it

def in_dining_room(r:item):
    # Function to check if the item is in the dining room
    symbol is_in_dining= exists room: item : (is_dining_room(room) and inside(r, dining_room))
    return is_in_dining

behavior start_ironing(char:character, iron:item, shirt:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(iron)
        # Turn on the iron
        achieve_once close_char(char, ironing_board)
        # Move close to the ironing board
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Ensure the shirt is on the ironing board
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        # Ensure the iron is plugged
        achieve_once on(iron, shirt)
        # Iron the shirt by placing the iron on it

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room]==41

        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and clean(shirt)
        
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and in_dining_room(iron)

        locate_iron(dining_room)
        start_ironing(char, iron, shirt, ironing_board)

#goal_representation
 
def in_dining_room(bowl:item):
    # Function to check if a bowl is in the dining room
    symbol in_dining_room = exists room: item : (is_dining_room(room) and inside(bowl, room))
    return in_dining_room

behavior locate_iron(dining_room:item, bowl:item, iron:item):
    body:
        observe(dining_room,"Find bowl with iron on it")
        # Ensure the dining room and bowl with iron is identified
        achieve_once inside(iron, dining_room) and on(iron, bowl)
        # Iron should be located on the specified bowl within the dining room

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item, sink:item, faucet:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inhand(shirt)
        achieve close_char(char, sink)
        achieve_once is_off(faucet)
        # Make sure the faucet is turned off before washing
        achieve clean(shirt)
        achieve has_water(shirt)

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, ironing_board:item, iron:item):
    body:
        achieve on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve_once is_on(iron)
        achieve close_char(char, ironing_board)
        achieve_once inhand(iron)
        # Youll need the iron inhand to iron the shirt
        achieve_once is_off(iron)
        # Assume iron is safely turned off after use

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room)

        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and in_dining_room(bowl) and id[bowl] == 2142

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and inside(iron, dining_room) and on(iron, bowl)

        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and id[shirt]==2158

        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink) and id[sink] == 20

        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet) and id[faucet] == 20

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board) and id[ironing_board] == 2144

        locate_iron(dining_room, bowl, iron)
        wash_shirt(shirt, sink, faucet)
        iron_shirt(shirt, ironing_board, iron)

#goal_representation_end

def find_iron(iron:item, bowl:item, dining_room:item):
    # Check if the iron is on the specified bowl inside the dining room
    symbol correct_bowl = exists o: item : (on(iron, o) and id[o] == id[bowl] and inside(o, dining_room))
    return correct_bowl

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(shirt)
        achieve has_water(shirt)

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        achieve is_on(iron)
        achieve_once clean(shirt)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room]==41
        # Find dining room by ID
        
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and id[bowl]==2142
        # Find bowl by ID
        
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron]==2161
        # Find iron by ID
        
        if not find_iron(iron, bowl, dining_room):
            # If iron is not found on the bowl, check other items in the dining room
            foreach b: item:
                if is_bowl(b) and not visited(b):
                    observe(b, "Check if iron is on this bowl")
        
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and id[shirt]==2158
        # Find the shirt by ID

        wash_shirt(shirt)
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board) and id[ironing_board]==2144
        iron_shirt(shirt, iron, ironing_board)

behavior locate_iron_in_dining_room():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room] == 41
        # Select the dining room with ID 41
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and id[bowl] == 2142 and inside(bowl, dining_room)
        # Select the bowl with ID 2142 inside the dining room
        observe(bowl, "Check if iron_2161 is on top of the bowl")
        # Observe the bowl to ensure iron_2161 is on top of it

behavior setup_ironing():
    body:
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron] == 2161
        # Select the iron with ID 2161
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board) and id[ironing_board] == 2144
        # Select the ironing board with ID 2144
        achieve_once on(iron, ironing_board)
        # Ensure the iron is on the ironing board
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Ensure the iron is turned on

def is_shirt_wet(shirt:item):
    # Function to check if a shirt is wet
    symbol has_water=exists water: item : (has_water(shirt))
    return has_water

behavior hand_wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        if not is_shirt_wet(shirt):
            bind faucet: item where:
                is_faucet(faucet) and id[faucet] == 20
            # Select the faucet with ID 20
            achieve has_water(shirt)
            # Ensure the shirt is wet

        wash(shirt)
        # Hand wash the shirt
        rinse(shirt)
        # Rinse the shirt
        achieve clean(shirt)
        # Ensure the shirt is clean

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Ensure the shirt is placed on the ironing board
        achieve_once plugged(iron)
        # Ensure the iron is plugged in
        push(iron)
        pull(iron)
        # Iron the shirt by pushing and pulling the iron over it

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and id[shirt] == 2158
        # Select the shirt with ID 2158
        
        hand_wash_shirt(shirt)
        # Hand wash the shirt
        
        locate_iron_in_dining_room()
        # Locate the iron in the dining room

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Bind ironing board for ironing shirt

        setup_ironing()
        # Prepare the iron and ironing board for the shirt
        
        iron_shirt(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Iron the shirt

#goal_representation_end

behavior find_iron_2161_around_home_office_241(iron:item):
    goal: not unknown(iron)
    body:
        assert is_iron(iron)
        bind home_office_instance:item where:
            is_home_office(home_office_instance) and id[home_office_instance]==241
        achieve close_char(char,home_office_instance)
        if can_open(home_office_instance):
            achieve_once open(home_office_instance)

def find_iron_and_bowl(iron:item, bowl:item):
    observe(dining_room,"Check for iron and bowl in the dining room")
    observe(bowl,"Check if iron is on top of the bowl")

behavior prepare_for_ironing():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        achieve clean(shirt)
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)

behavior switch_on_iron_and_iron_shirt(iron:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(iron)
        achieve clean(clothes_shirt_2158) # To ensure the shirt is properly ironed it must be clean
        # Iron the shirt placed on the ironing board

behavior placing_iron_on_bowl(iron:item, bowl:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(iron, bowl)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room)
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and inside(iron, dining_room)
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and inside(bowl, dining_room)
        if not (visited(iron) and visited(bowl)):
            find_iron_and_bowl(iron, bowl)
        prepare_for_ironing()
        switch_on_iron_and_iron_shirt(iron)
        placing_iron_on_bowl(iron, bowl)

behavior find_iron_bowl(dining_room:item, bowl:item, iron:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(iron, dining_room)
        # Ensure the iron is in the dining room
        achieve_once on(iron, bowl)
        # Ensure the iron is on the bowl
        achieve_once inside(bowl, dining_room)
        # Ensure the bowl is in the dining room

def is_ready_to_iron(item:item):
    # Check if the iron is plugged in and on
    symbol ready=plugged(item) and is_on(item)
    return ready

behavior prepare_shirt_for_ironing(clothes_shirt:item, sink:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(clothes_shirt) # Ensure the shirt is clean
        achieve_once inside(clothes_shirt, sink) # Place the shirt in the sink
        wash(clothes_shirt) # Wash the shirt
        rinse(clothes_shirt) # Rinse the shirt
        achieve_once on(clothes_shirt, ironing_board) # Place the shirt on the ironing board

behavior use_iron_on_shirt(iron:item, clothes_shirt:item):
    body:
        if is_ready_to_iron(iron):
            push(iron) # Push the iron across the shirt
            pull(iron) # Pull the iron across the shirt
        else:
            achieve is_on(iron) # Turn on the iron
            push(iron) # Push the iron across the shirt
            pull(iron) # Pull the iron across the shirt

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room)
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl)
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron)
        bind clothes_shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(clothes_shirt)
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        
        find_iron_bowl(dining_room, bowl, iron)
        prepare_shirt_for_ironing(clothes_shirt, sink, ironing_board)
        use_iron_on_shirt(iron, clothes_shirt)

def locate_iron():
    # Function to help locate the iron in the dining room
    bind dining_room: item where:
        is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room] == 41
    bind bowl_2142: item where:
        is_bowl(bowl_2142) and inside(bowl_2142, dining_room)
    observe(bowl_2142, "Check if iron_2161 is on top")

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        wash(shirt)
        rinse(shirt)
        # Wash and rinse the shirt

behavior prepare_for_ironing(shirt:item, ironing_board:item, iron:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve close_char(char, iron)
        achieve_once inhand(iron)
        touch(iron) # Turn on the iron
        achieve is_on(iron)

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, ironing_board:item):
    body:
        achieve on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve close_char(char, iron)
        push(iron)
        pull(iron)
        # Iron the shirt by pushing and pulling the iron on it

        # Locate iron

    body:
        achieve inside_char(char, dining_room)
        observe(bowl, "Check is iron on the bowl")
        if not visited(iron):
            observe(iron, "Is iron on the bowl")

        achieve_once on(shirt, ironing_board)
        achieve is_on(iron)
        achieve clean(shirt)

behavior pick_up_iron(iron:item, bowl:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(iron, bowl) 
        # Move the iron from the bowl to be picked up

behavior wash_shirt(shirt:item):
    body:
        achieve clean(shirt)
        achieve has_water(shirt)

behavior iron_shirt(shirt:item, board:item, iron:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, board) 
        # Place the shirt on the ironing board
        achieve is_on(iron)
        achieve_once on(iron, shirt)
        # Iron is used on the shirt

        # Obtain the ironing board with ID 2144

#goal_representation
 
def is_on_correct_bowl(iron:item, bowl:item):
    # Function to check if iron is on the specified bowl
    symbol correct_bowl=exists o: item : (id[o]==bowl and on(iron, o))
    return correct_bowl

behavior find_iron_on_bowl(bowl:item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, bowl)
        # Ensure the character is close to the correct bowl to find the iron
        observe(bowl, "Check if iron is on this bowl")
        # Observe the bowl to verify irons presence

behavior find_and_collect_iron_bowl_2142():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room) and id[dining_room] == 41
        bind bowl: item where:
            is_bowl(bowl) and id[bowl] == 2142
        # Make sure to check this specific bowl
        
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and inside(iron, dining_room)
        if is_on_correct_bowl(iron, bowl):
            find_iron_on_bowl(bowl)
        else:
            foreach b: item:
                if is_bowl(b) and not visited(b):
                    find_iron_on_bowl(b)
        # Check all unvisited bowls for the iron

behavior wash_rinse_shirt(shirt:item, faucet:item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, faucet)
        wash(shirt)
        rinse(shirt)

behavior place_shirt_on_ironing_board(shirt:item, board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once on(shirt, board)

behavior iron_the_shirt(shirt:item, iron:item, board:item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, iron)
        achieve plugged(iron)
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Ensure iron is on and plugged in before using
        achieve_once on(iron, shirt)
        # Iron the shirt by placing the iron on it
        achieve unplugged(iron)
        achieve is_off(iron)
        # Turn off and unplug iron after use

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt) and id[shirt] == 2158
        bind faucet: item where:
            is_faucet(faucet) and id[faucet] == 20
        wash_rinse_shirt(shirt, faucet)
        
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board) and id[ironing_board] == 2144
        place_shirt_on_ironing_board(shirt, ironing_board)

        find_and_collect_iron_bowl_2142()

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron] == 2161
        iron_the_shirt(shirt, iron, ironing_board)

#goal_representation_end
